\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01732}01732\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01733}01733\ \ \ \ \ sys.path\_importer\_cache\ contains\ finder\ objects\ that\ have\ been\ cached\ when}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01734}01734\ \ \ \ \ importing\ data\ from\ the\ original\ distribution.\ Any\ such\ finders\ need\ to\ be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01735}01735\ \ \ \ \ cleared\ since\ the\ replacement\ distribution\ might\ be\ packaged\ differently,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01736}01736\ \ \ \ \ e.g.\ a\ zipped\ egg\ distribution\ might\ get\ replaced\ with\ an\ unzipped\ egg}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01737}01737\ \ \ \ \ folder\ or\ vice\ versa.\ Having\ the\ old\ finders\ cached\ may\ then\ cause\ Python}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01738}01738\ \ \ \ \ to\ attempt\ loading\ modules\ from\ the\ replacement\ distribution\ using\ an}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01739}01739\ \ \ \ \ incorrect\ loader.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01740}01740\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01741}01741\ \ \ \ \ zipimport.zipimporter\ objects\ are\ Python\ loaders\ charged\ with\ importing}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01742}01742\ \ \ \ \ data\ packaged\ inside\ zip\ archives.\ If\ stale\ loaders\ referencing\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01743}01743\ \ \ \ \ original\ distribution,\ are\ left\ behind,\ they\ can\ fail\ to\ load\ modules\ from}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01744}01744\ \ \ \ \ the\ replacement\ distribution.\ E.g.\ if\ an\ old\ zipimport.zipimporter\ instance}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01745}01745\ \ \ \ \ is\ used\ to\ load\ data\ from\ a\ new\ zipped\ egg\ archive,\ it\ may\ cause\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01746}01746\ \ \ \ \ operation\ to\ attempt\ to\ locate\ the\ requested\ data\ in\ the\ wrong\ location\ -\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01747}01747\ \ \ \ \ one\ indicated\ by\ the\ original\ distribution's\ zip\ archive\ directory}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01748}01748\ \ \ \ \ information.\ Such\ an\ operation\ may\ then\ fail\ outright,\ e.g.\ report\ having}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01749}01749\ \ \ \ \ read\ a\ 'bad\ local\ file\ header',\ or\ even\ worse,\ it\ may\ fail\ silently\ \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01750}01750\ \ \ \ \ return\ invalid\ data.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01751}01751\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01752}01752\ \ \ \ \ zipimport.\_zip\_directory\_cache\ contains\ cached\ zip\ archive\ directory}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01757}01757\ \ \ \ \ If\ asked,\ and\ the\ underlying\ Python\ implementation\ allows\ it,\ we\ can\ fix}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01758}01758\ \ \ \ \ all\ existing\ zipimport.zipimporter\ instances\ instead\ of\ having\ to\ track}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01759}01759\ \ \ \ \ them\ down\ and\ remove\ them\ one\ by\ one,\ by\ updating\ their\ shared\ cached\ zip}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01762}01762\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01763}01763\ \ \ \ \ If\ not\ asked\ to\ fix\ existing\ zipimport.zipimporter\ instances,\ we\ still\ do}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01764}01764\ \ \ \ \ our\ best\ to\ clear\ any\ remaining\ zipimport.zipimporter\ related\ cached\ data}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01765}01765\ \ \ \ \ that\ might\ somehow\ later\ get\ used\ when\ attempting\ to\ load\ data\ from\ the\ new}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01766}01766\ \ \ \ \ distribution\ and\ thus\ cause\ such\ load\ operations\ to\ fail.\ Note\ that\ when}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01767}01767\ \ \ \ \ tracking\ down\ such\ remaining\ stale\ data,\ we\ can\ not\ catch\ every\ conceivable}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01768}01768\ \ \ \ \ usage\ from\ here,\ and\ we\ clear\ only\ those\ that\ we\ know\ of\ and\ have\ found\ to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01769}01769\ \ \ \ \ cause\ problems\ if\ left\ alive.\ Any\ remaining\ caches\ should\ be\ updated\ by}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01770}01770\ \ \ \ \ whomever\ is\ in\ charge\ of\ maintaining\ them,\ i.e.\ they\ should\ be\ ready\ to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01771}01771\ \ \ \ \ handle\ us\ replacing\ their\ zip\ archives\ with\ new\ distributions\ at\ runtime.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01772}01772\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01773}01773\ \ \ \ \ "{}"{}"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01774}01774\ \ \ \ \ \#\ There\ are\ several\ other\ known\ sources\ of\ stale\ zipimport.zipimporter}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01775}01775\ \ \ \ \ \#\ instances\ that\ we\ do\ not\ clear\ here,\ but\ might\ if\ ever\ given\ a\ reason\ to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01776}01776\ \ \ \ \ \#\ do\ so:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01777}01777\ \ \ \ \ \#\ *\ Global\ setuptools\ pkg\_resources.working\_set\ (a.k.a.\ 'master\ working}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{easy__install_8py_source_l01784}01784\ \ \ \ \ \#\ \ \ that\ this\ information\ is\ intended\ mostly\ for\ introspection\ and\ so\ is}
